    INNER JOIN [Sizes] AS [dtoBillDetail.Size0] ON [x.BillDetails0].[SizeId] = [dtoBillDetail.Size0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [dtoBillDetail.Product0] ON [x.BillDetails0].[ProductId] = [dtoBillDetail.Product0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [ProductCategories] AS [dtoBillDetail.Product.ProductCategory0] ON [dtoBillDetail.Product0].[CategoryId] = [dtoBillDetail.Product.ProductCategory0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [dtoBillDetail.Color0] ON [x.BillDetails0].[ColorId] = [dtoBillDetail.Color0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [x1].[DateCreated], [x1].[Id]
        FROM [Bills] AS [x1]
        ORDER BY [x1].[DateCreated] DESC, [x1].[Id]
        OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
    ) AS [t0] ON [x.BillDetails0].[BillId] = [t0].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [dtoBillDetail.Product.ProductCategory.Products].[CategoryId] = [t1].[Id1]
